<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсия</a> (2497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pensio</i>.
Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пансион.html>пансио́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pansion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pénsija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенсия.html>пе́нсий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pension</li>
<li>retirement</li></ol>

<p>Via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from an Indo-Aryan language. </p>

***пенять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенять.html>пеня́ть</a> (16967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пеня.html>пе́ня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pénja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенять.html>пеня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">penjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">попеня́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reproach <i>(with)</i>, to blame
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенять.html>пеня́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">penjáj na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you alone are to blame; you have only yourself to  blame</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зеркало.html>зе́ркало</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенять.html>пеня́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кривой.html>крива́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">néčevo na zérkalo penjátʹ, koli róža krivá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> don't lay your own faults at another person's door; don't blame your own faults on others</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:первенство.html>пе́рвенство</a> (11182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первенство.html>пе́рвенство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pérvenstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первенство.html>пе́рвенства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первенство.html>пе́рвенства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первенство.html>пе́рвенств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>first place, top ranking</li>
<li>priority</li>
<li>championship

***первопричина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:первопричина.html>первопричи́на</a> (27410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pérvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причина.html>причи́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pričína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первопричина.html>первопричи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pervopričína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первопричина.html>первопричи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первопричина.html>первопричи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первопричина.html>первопричи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> original / initial chaos, the beginning</li>
<li>first cause, prime cause</li></ol>

***первый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a> (79)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pьrvъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">first</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*pírˀwas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pr̥h₂wós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pérvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>first
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pérvyj</b> denʹ nedéli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>first</b> day of the week</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>chief, main</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пе́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a>, адъективное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-перв-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***перебегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a> (11384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run <i>(across)</i>, to cross <i>(at a run [running])</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebegatʹ</b> na nóvoje mésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run to a new place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebegatʹ</b> dorógu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to steal a march on smb; snatch smth from under smb's nose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to move, to shift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebegatʹ</b> glazámi s predméta na predmét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shift one's eyes from one object to another; scan one's surroundings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсвет.html>о́тсветы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:костер.html>костра́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебегали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>ли́цам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ótsvety kostrá perebegali po lícam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the light of the fire flickered on their faces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to defect <i>(to)</i>, to go over <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́телю</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebegatʹ</b> k neprijátelju; <b>perebegatʹ</b> na stóronu protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to desert to the enemy; turn traitor</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***перебежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a> (10628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run <i>(across)</i>, to cross <i>(at a run [running])</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> čerez dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run across the road</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> úlicu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run across the street; cross the street (running)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> na nóvoje mésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run to a new place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> dorógu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to steal a march on smb; snatch smth from under smb's nose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to move, to shift</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to defect <i>(to)</i>, to go over <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́телю</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> k neprijátelju; perebegatʹ na stóronu protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to desert to the enemy; turn traitor</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
